MISC_158;Make 10 misplays in a single Kaycee's Mod run.;在凱茜的模組中，於一輪遊戲內犯下10次失誤。
MISC_676;Pulling Teeth;拔牙
MISC_643;Pull out 32 teeth in Kaycee's Mod.;在凱茜的模組中，拔下 32 顆牙齒。
MISC_619;Bad Moon;惡月高掛
MISC_245;Defeat Leshy in Kaycee's Mod without destroying The Moon.;在凱茜的模組中擊敗雷希，且不摧毀月亮。
CREATEEGG_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_602;When a card bearing this sigil is played, an Egg is created on the opposing space.;在打出有此印記的卡牌後，一顆蛋會出現在對面的格子。
DOUBLESTRIKE_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_275;A card bearing this sigil will strike the opposing space an extra time when attacking.;有此印記的卡牌在攻擊時會朝對面的位置額外攻擊一次。
GAINATTACKONKILL_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_163;When a card bearing this sigil attacks an opposing creature and it perishes, this card gains 1 power.;有此印記的卡牌在攻擊對面生物且殺死對方後，將提升 1 點攻擊力。
HYDRAEGG_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_095;A card bearing this sigil hatches when drawn if the numbers 1 to 5 are represented in the health of creatures in your deck, and in their power, and if there is a creature of each tribe in your deck.;有此印記的卡牌會在滿足特定條件下孵化。條件一是牌組中的卡牌要包含 1 到 5 點的生命力和攻擊力；條件二是牌組中要有各種族類的生物至少一隻。
MADEOFSTONE_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_046;A card bearing this sigil is immune to the effects of Touch of Death and Stinky.;有此印記的卡牌免疫死亡之觸和臭味的效果。
MORSEL_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_754;When a card bearing this sigil is sacrificed, it adds its stat values to the card it was sacrificed for.;在犧牲有此印記的卡牌時，其能力數值會加算到以此犧牲召喚出的卡牌上。
OPPONENTBONES_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_456;While a card bearing this sigil is on the board, opposing creatures also provide bones when perishing.;當有此印記的卡牌在牌桌上，對手生物死亡後也會給予我方骨頭。
STRAFESWAP_RULEBOOKDESCRIPTION_C_364;At the end of the owner's turn, a card bearing this sigil will move in the direction inscribed in the sigil. Creatures in the way will be thrown back behind it.;在擁有者的回合結束時，有此印記的卡牌會朝印記顯示的方向移動。擋在路上的生物會被撞到它後面。
BONESSTATICON_GBCDESCRIPTION_C_426;The power of a card bearing this sigil is equal to half of the Bones of the owner.;有此印記的卡牌攻擊力等同於擁有者的骨頭數量的一半。
